# BIDS-Dandisets Dashboard
A simple dashboard for displaying the successes or failures of running nwb2bids on a Dandiset.
### Summary
|  Dandisets Successfully Converted  |  Passing `nwb2bids` Inspection  |  Passing BIDS Validation  |
| :--------------------------------: | :-----------------------------: | :-----------------------: |
|         696 / 723 (96.3%)          |        544 / 696 (78.2%)        |     243 / 696 (33.6%)     |
